Too many comments are written and no one reads it. So let‚Äôs just comment briefly and focus on the key points üòÇ This time I stayed in the boutique executive suite of the InterContinental Hotel, and an upgrade was made at the front desk when checking in. The day before check-in, the lady's birthday was noted in advance. Miss Kylie from the Guest Relations Depar**ent brought us a 1 pound cheesecakeüç∞ and a handwritten card. The interior of the guest room was also simply furnished. Thank you. Immediately after checking in, I went to Spain, a hot spot on the third floor, in exchange for my member's welcome drink ü§£GinTonic is very refreshing, I like it very much üíïAs the only Forbes five-star Intercontinental hotel in China, it is indeed the best choice for business travel and city vacation! ü§£ü§£ü§£

Afternoon Tea: Executive benefits include one afternoon tea for two. The place to eat is on the 22nd floor of Club InterContinental. The salty finger sandwiches are not bad. The remaining two layers of desserts are average. I have to complain about SconeüòÖ Although it is freshly baked, the taste and texture are real. . . After one bite, it was directly pasted on my upper gums with chewing üò≠ An uncomfortable batch. Praise the ice cream and orange juice, orange juice is not semi-finished but freshly squeezed. And the juicer and wine dispenser are still very advanced üëç Forgot to ask what brand they are ü§£ Meal time is from 2:30 to 5:00.

Happy hour: Happy hour at the club on the 22nd floor. Happy hour with free-flowing drinks and light meals. The food source should be the Ying Chinese buffet on the third floor. Although it is not delicious, it really solves the problem of dinner. For drinks, I ordered a glass of Ms. GinTonic and a glass of whiskey sore. . Meal time 6:00pm to 8:00pm ü§£

Hotel infrastructure: The guest room part does not show too many photos because there are personal items. The 70-square-meter room has a lot of space but the design is a little deformed. The cloakroom and luggage rack are relatively biased, and the bathroom and toilet are separated from wet and dry. The infrastructure is perfect, the mini bar is given free drinks on the first day, and the hotel has also changed to a new smart toilet. But I didn't see the three samples I expected. . . ü•≤ü•≤ü•≤

Swimming Pool & Gym: 5th floor of InterContinental Hotel. These two places won my heart and met my needs for three exercises a day. Morning exercise, afternoon fitness, evening swimming. If you are interested, you can click on the video to watch it üòÇ but I still have to complain about the serious falling of bricks in the swimming pool. While exercising, enjoy the night view of Sanlitun! ü§£üëç

Breakfast: Chinese food on the third floor of the InterContinental Hotel. I have been here before the restaurant week. But it was the first time to have breakfast here. The semi-buffet breakfast is quite rich in content. But compared to other domestic five-star luxury hotels. . . Slightly inferior üò≠ There are a few types of fried vegetables. The eggs Benedict looks pretty goodüëç Asked about it. . . Need a single point üòÇüòÇüòÇ

Executive benefits: afternoon tea for two, happy hour light meal and free flow of drinks, free laundry and ironing, late check-out at 4:00 pm, free use of gym and swimming pool, breakfast for two, free use of meeting room for 1 hourü§î

Summary of Disadvantages:
Question 1: The smart toilet in the bathroom will automatically turn on strangely at night. You can imagine that when you are sleepy, the bathroom suddenly lights upüôÑThe sound of the smart toilet opening the lidüò® can be imagined. . . It is recommended to repair the intelligent identification system so as not to disturb the rest of the guests.
Question two:
The bathroom bathroom shower switch is round. Usually, everyone will apply shampoo and shower gel after turning off the water. It's hard to turn on the shower switch when the hands are soaked with foam, it's too slippery and there is no friction at all. The towel I used at the end was barely openedüòßAlthough the design is for beauty, please also consider whether it is convenient to useü§î
Question 3: Summary of small problems
1. Is there really no three samples of washing and care? (ps. I'm the kind of person who prefers to take three samples away.) There are three large bottles of toiletries, and the quality control is ok. But something embarrassing still happened. The lady found out that the shampoo pump was broken in the middle of the bath and I immediately contacted the concierge.
2. The mosaic tiles of the swimming pool have fallen off seriously. There is a thicker grease covering on the stone piers in the spa area. Regular cleaning is recommended.
3. The location of the cloakroom and luggage rack is a bit off, not at the door of the guest room. The bathtub does not come with a disposable tub cover.
4. Because the room was booked on a certain journey, the hotel did not call in advance. The identity information was verified by contacting the hotel one day before my check-in (no pre-arrival service)

Praise: The check in at the front desk is very efficient and there is no waiting room. Kylie from the relations depar**ent presented welcome fruits, cakes and handwritten cards üí™ (it can be seen that the hotel management attaches great importance to customer birthdays, anniversaries, etc.) Because I am not used to sleeping with too soft pillows , so I contacted the concierge, and the buckwheat pillow and cassia pillow were delivered in less than 10 minutes. The service was very good.

Summary: Although the InterContinental Sanlitun is not the most luxurious in Beijing, it is indeed one of the most thoughtful hotels in Beijing that I have stayed in. Although the above evaluation is somewhat subjective and strict, any small problem for a hotel of this magnitude can become the direction of hotel improvement. I agreed to write a brief review, and at the end I wrote a lot of long-winded wordsüòÇ Finally, I hope that the InterContinental Hotel Sanlitun Tongying Center will do better and better!
